<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Item
8.01 Other Events</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">DALLAS, Texas, and CAESAREA,
Israel &ndash; Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. announces a new license agreement &ndash; &ldquo;New Megiddo 428&rdquo; &ndash; granted
over the previous Megiddo-Jezreel license area in northern Israel. </FONT>As of December 3, 2020, Israel&rsquo;s Petroleum Commissioner
granted Zion Oil &amp; Gas a new license agreement over the previous 99,000-acre license area. The term of the new license agreement
is for six months. Similar to previous Zion license agreements, Israel&rsquo;s Petroleum Commissioner has the authority to grant
the New Megiddo 428 license. The New Megiddo 428 license may be extended for an additional six months for a total license period
of twelve months.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<DESCRIPTION>PRESS RELEASE DATED DECEMBER 3, 2020
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>Zion Oil &amp; Gas Receives New Oil
and Gas Exploration License Agreement from Israel</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>Zion drilling crew works to finish
rig assembly at drill site for inspections.</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black; background-color: white">DALLAS, Texas,
and CAESAREA, Israel, December 3, 2020 /PRNewswire/&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="color: Black">Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. <FONT STYLE="background-color: white">(OTCQX:
ZNOG) announces a new license agreement &ndash; &ldquo;New Megiddo 428&rdquo; &ndash; granted over the previous Megiddo-Jezreel
license area in northern Israel. </FONT></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&ldquo;We are thankful for Israel&rsquo;s
unwavering support during these unprecedented times,&rdquo; stated Zion Oil &amp; Gas CEO, Robert Dunn. &ldquo;Receiving a new
license will allow Zion&rsquo;s operations to continue drilling into 2021.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>NEW LICENSE AGREEMENT &ndash; &ldquo;NEW
MEGGIDO 428&rdquo;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">As of December 3, 2020, Israel&rsquo;s
Petroleum Commissioner granted Zion Oil &amp; Gas a new license agreement from the State of Israel over the previous 99,000-acre
license area.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">The term of the new license agreement
has been granted for six months.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">Similar to previous Zion license agreements
Israel&rsquo;s Petroleum Commissioner has the authority to grant the New Megiddo 428 license.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">The New Megiddo 428 license may be extended
for an additional six months for a total license period of twelve months.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 264pt; width: 5in"></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><I>Zion Oil &amp;
Gas License Area</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"></P>



<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>OPERATIONAL HIGHLIGHTS</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&ldquo;Operationally, everything is
coming together as planned,&rdquo; Zion's VP of Operations, Monty Kness, expressed. &ldquo;The crew morale is high and we&rsquo;re
all looking forward to spudding soon.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">All necessary drilling equipment and
supplies have either arrived at the rig site or are in port going through final clearance procedures.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">The drilling crew is working diligently
to assemble the rig in time for Israeli governmental inspections which are scheduled for next week.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"></FONT></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo --><!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><IMG SRC="image_002.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 269.25pt; width: 5in"></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><I>Zion rig and
equipment loaded onto trucks at Haifa port on November 23 (top left),<BR>
Zion rig being assembled on pad site on November 24 (top right),</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><I>Zion Drilling
crew on December 2 (bottom left), </I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><I>Zion drill site
location with equipment on December 2 (bottom right)</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black; background-color: white">Zion Oil &amp;
Gas, a public company, traded on OTCQX Best Market, explores for oil and gas onshore in Israel on their 99,000-acre Megiddo-Jezreel
license area. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><I>&ldquo;The Lord
Himself goes before you and will be with you; He will never leave you nor forsake you. Do not be afraid; do not be discouraged.&rdquo;
</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><I>Deuteronomy 31:8</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><I>&ldquo;Sing to

great is the Holy One of Israel among you.&rdquo; </I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="color: Black"><I>Isaiah 12:5-6</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="color: Black; background-color: white">FORWARD-LOOKING
STATEMENTS: Statements in this communication that are not historical fact, including, but not limited to, statements regarding
Zion&rsquo;s operations; Zion&rsquo;s ability to continue as a going concern; operational risks in ongoing exploration efforts;
the timing and completion of the processing, interpretation of the results and plans contingent thereon off the 3-D seismic survey;
regulatory approvals needed for the rig&rsquo;s erection, start-up, and operation; the effect, if any, of the coronavirus pandemic
on the timing of the delivery, start-up and operation of the well, and liquidity for shareholders on OTCQX are forward-looking
statements as defined in the &ldquo;Safe Harbor&rdquo; provisions of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. These
forward-looking statements are based on assumptions that are subject to significant known and unknown risks, uncertainties, and
other unpredictable factors, many of which are described in Zion&rsquo;s periodic reports filed with the SEC and are beyond Zion&rsquo;s

statements. These risks and uncertainties include, but are not limited to, those described in Item 1A in Zion&rsquo;s Annual Report

filings with the SEC. Zion can give no assurance that the expectations reflected in these statements will prove to be correct
and assumes no responsibility to update these statements.</FONT></P>
